<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">seide</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">seid</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">iseid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sǣde</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sæġde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġesæġd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:say.html>say</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ed</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi"><a href = vnd.unilang:hindi.html>Hindi</a></a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindustani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hindustani language">Hindustani</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">سَائِس</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sāʾis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stableman, <a href = vnd.unilang:groom.html>groom</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">سَاس</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sās</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> tend <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horse.html>horse</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sak.html>sak</a> (88545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">sǫk</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sakō</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nynorsk" class="extiw" title="w:Nynorsk">Norwegian Nynorsk</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:sak.html>sak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:sag.html>sag</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">sök</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sake.html>sake</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sache</i>.

			<div class="gallerytext">
<p>3. <a href = vnd.unilang:essentieel.html>essentiële</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:echte.html>echte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:salie.html>salie</a></b>"

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:salontafel.html>salontafel</a> (34717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:salon.html>salon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sam-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:prefix.html>prefix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sām-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">half-; <a href = vnd.unilang:partly.html>partly</a>; incompletely</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sēmi-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sēmi-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>Related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">semi-</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span>).

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenvatten.html>samenvatten</a> (21243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
